Unique subsets (based on subset name) are concatenated to the original rule's list of subsets\n    35→// 2. If the original rule did not have any top level traffic policy, traffic policies from the new rule will be\n    36→// used.\n    37→// 3. If the original rule did not have any exportTo, exportTo settings from the new rule will be used.\n    38→func (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig destRuleConfig.Meta)\n    41→\tif mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n    42→\t\t// `addRuleToProcessedDestRules` determines if the incoming destination rule would become a new unique entry in the processedDestRules list.\n    43→\t\taddRuleToProcessedDestRules := true\n    44→\t\tfor i, mdr := range mdrList {\n    45→\t\t\texistingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n    46→\t\t\tbothWithoutSelector := rule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil && existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil\n    47→\t\t\tbothWithSelector := existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil\n    48→\t\t\tselectorsMatch := labels.Instance(existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels()).Equals(rule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n    49→\n    50→\t\t\tif bothWithSelector && !selectorsMatch {\n    51→\t\t\t\t// If the new destination rule and the existing one has workload selectors associated with them, skip merging\n    52→\t\t\t\t// if the selectors do not match\n    53→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n    54→\t\t\t}\n    55→\n    56→\t\t\t// If both the destination rules are without a workload selector or with matching workload selectors, simply merge them.\n    57→\t\t\t// If the incoming rule has a workload selector, it has to be merged with the existing rules with workload selector, and\n    58→\t\t\t// at the same time added as a unique entry in the processedDestRules.\n    59→\t\t\tif bothWithoutSelector || (rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && selectorsMatch) {\n    60→\t\t\t\taddRuleToProcessedDestRules = false\n    61→\t\t\t}\n    62→\n    63→\t\t\t// Deep copy destination rule, to prevent mutate it later when merge with a new one.\n    64→\t\t\t// This can happen when there are more than one destination rule of same host in one namespace.\n    65→\t\t\tcopied := mdr.DeepCopy()\n    66→\t\t\tp.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied\n    67→\t\t\tmergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n    68→\n    69→\t\t\texistingSubset := map[string]struct{}{}\n    70→\t\t\tfor _, subset := range mergedRule.Subsets {\n    71→\t\t\t\texistingSubset[subset.Name] = struct{}{}\n    72→\t\t\t}\n    73→\t\t\t// we have an another destination rule for same host.\n    74→\t\t\t// concatenate both of them -- essentially add subsets from one to other.\n    75→\t\t\t// Note: we only add the subsets and do not overwrite anything else like exportTo or top level\n    76→\t\t\t// traffic policies if they already exist\n    77→\t\t\tfor _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n    78→\t\t\t\tif _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n    79→\t\t\t\t\t// if not duplicated, append\n    80→\t\t\t\t\tmergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n    81→\t\t\t\t} else {\n    82→\t\t\t\t\t// duplicate subset\n    83→\t\t\t\t\tps.AddMetric(DuplicatedSubsets, string(resolvedHost), \"\",\n    84→\t\t\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"Duplicate subset %s found while merging destination rules for %s\",\n    85→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tsubset.Name, string(resolvedHost)))\n    86→\t\t\t\t}\n    87→\t\t\t}\n    88→\n    89→\t\t\t// If there is no top level policy and the incoming rule has top level\n    90→\t\t\t// traffic policy, use the one from the incoming rule.\n    91→\t\t\tif mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n    92→\t\t\t\tmergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n    93→\t\t\t}\n    94→\t\t\t// If there is no exportTo in the existing rule and\n    95→\t\t\t// the incoming rule has an explicit exportTo, use the\n    96→\t\t\t// one from the incoming rule.\n    97→\t\t\tif len(p.exportTo[resolvedHost]) == 0 && len(exportToMap) > 0 {\n    98→\t\t\t\tp.exportTo[resolvedHost] = exportToMap\n    99→\t\t\t}\n   100→\t\t}\n   101→\t\tif addRuleToProcessedDestRules {\n   102→\t\t\tp.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n   103→\t\t}\n   104→\t\treturn\n   105→\t}\n   106→\t// DestinationRule does not exist for the resolved host so add it\n   107→\tp.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n   108→\tp.exportTo[resolvedHost] = exportToMap\n   109→}\n   110→\n   111→// inheritDestinationRule child config inherits settings from parent mesh/namespace\n   112→func (ps *PushContext) inheritDestinationRule(parent, child *config.Config) *config.Config {\n   113→\tif parent == nil {\n   114→\t\treturn child\n   115→\t}\n   116→\tif child == nil {\n   117→\t\treturn parent\n   118→\t}\n   119→\n   120→\tparentDR := parent.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n   121→\tif parentDR.TrafficPolicy == nil {\n   122→\t\treturn child\n   123→\t}\n   124→\n   125→\tmerged := parent.DeepCopy()\n   126→\t// merge child into parent, child fields will overwrite Note that it does not perform inheritance style merging.\n// IOW, given three dest rules (*.foo.com, *.foo.com, *.com), calling this function for\n// each config will result in a final dest rule set (*.foo.com, and *.com).\n//\n// The following is the merge logic:\n// 1. Unique subsets (based on subset name) are concatenated to the original rule's list of subsets\n// 2. If the original rule did not have any top level traffic policy, traffic policies from the new rule will be\n// used.\n// 3. If the original rule did not have any exportTo, exportTo settings from the new rule will be used.\nfunc (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, exportToMap map[visibility.Instance]bool) {\n\trule := destRuleConfig.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\tresolvedHost := ResolveShortnameToFQDN(rule.Host, destRuleConfig.Meta)\n\tif mdrList, exists list.\n\t\taddRuleToProcessedDestRules := true\n\t\tfor i, mdr := range mdrList {\n\t\t\texistingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\t\t\tbothWithoutSelector := rule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil && existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil\n\t\t\tbothWithSelector := existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil\n\t\t\tselectorsMatch := labels.Instance(existingRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels()).Equals(rule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n\n\t\t\tif bothWithSelector && !selectorsMatch {\n\t\t\t\t// If the new destination rule and the existing one has workload selectors associated with them, skip merging\n\t\t\t\t// if the selectors do not match\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// If both the destination rules are without a workload selector or with matching workload selectors, simply merge them.\n\t\t\t// If the incoming rule has a workload selector, it has to be merged with the existing rules with workload selector, and\n\t\t\t// at the same time added as a unique entry in the processedDestRules.\n\t\t\tif bothWithoutSelector || (rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && selectorsMatch) {\n\t\t\t\taddRuleToProcessedDestRules = false\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Deep copy destination rule, to prevent mutate it later when merge with a new one.\n\t\t\t// This can happen when there are more than one destination rule of same host in one namespace.\n\t\t\tcopied := mdr.DeepCopy()\n\t\t\tp.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied\n\t\t\tmergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\n\t\t\texistingSubset := map[string]struct{}{}\n\t\t\tfor _, subset := range mergedRule.Subsets {\n\t\t\t\texistingSubset[subset.Name] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// we have an another destination rule for same host.\n\t\t\t// concatenate both of them -- essentially add subsets from one to other.\n\t\t\t// Note: we only add the subsets and do not overwrite anything else like exportTo or top level\n\t\t\t// traffic policies if they already exist\n\t\t\tfor _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n\t\t\t\tif _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t// if not duplicated, append\n\t\t\t\t\tmergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\t// duplicate subset\n\t\t\t\t\tps.AddMetric(DuplicatedSubsets, string(resolvedHost), \"\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"Duplicate subset %s found while merging destination rules for %s\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tsubset.Name, string(resolvedHost)))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// If there is no top level policy and the incoming rule has top level\n\t\t\t// traffic policy, use the one from the incoming rule.\n\t\t\tif mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n\t\t\t\tmergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// If there is no exportTo in the existing rule and\n\t\t\t// the incoming rule has an explicit exportTo, use the\n\t\t\t// one from the incoming rule.\n\t\t\tif len(p.exportTo[resolvedHost]) == 0 && len(exportToMap) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tp.exportTo[resolvedHost] = exportToMap\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif addRuleToProcessedDestRules {\n\t\t\tp.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\t// DestinationRule does not exist for the resolved host so add it\n\tp.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n\tp.exportTo[resolvedHost] = exportToMap\n}\n\n// inheritDestinationRule child config inherits settings from parent mesh/namespace\nfunc (ps *PushContext) inheritDestinationRule(parent, child *config.Config) *config.Config {\n\tif parent == nil Precomputing the list of services, virtual services, dest rules\n    59→// for a sidecar improves performance as we no longer need to compute this\n    60→// list for every sidecar. 263→\t\tSidecar:            sidecar,\n   264→\t\tconfigDependencies: make(map[uint64]struct{}),\n   265→\t\tRootNamespace:      ps.Mesh.RootNamespace,\n   266→\t\tVersion:            ps.PushVersion,\n the svc in slice\n   292→\t}\n   293→\tservicesAdded := make(map[host.Name]serviceIndex)\n   294→\taddService := func(s *Service) {\n   295→\t\tif s == nil {\n   296→\t\t\treturn\n   297→\t\t}\n   298→\t\tif foundSvc, found := servicesAdded[s.Hostname]; !found {\n   299→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   300→\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.ServiceEntry,\n   301→\t\t\t\tName: len(out.services) - 1}\n   306→\t\t} else if foundSvc.svc.Attributes.Namespace == s.Attributes.Namespace && s.Ports != nil && len(s.Ports) > 0 {\n   307→\t\t\t// merge the ports to service when each listener generates partial service\n   308→\t\t\t// we only merge if the found service is in the same namespace as the one we're trying to add\n   309→\t\t\tcopied := foundSvc.svc.DeepCopy()\n   310→\t\t\tfor _, p := range s.Ports {\n   311→\t\t\t\tfound := false\n   312→\t\t\t\tfor _, osp := range copied.Ports {\n   313→\t\t\t\t\tif p.Port == osp.Port {\n   314→\t\t\t\t\t\tfound = true\n   315→\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   316→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   317→\t\t\t\t}\n   318→\t\t\t\tif !found {\n   319→\t\t\t\t\tcopied.Ports = append(copied.Ports, p)\n   320→\t\t\t\t}\n   321→\t\t\t}\n   322→\t\t\t// explicitly requested services, which take priority\n   329→\t\tfor _, s := range listener.services {\n   330→\t\t\taddService(s)\n   331→\t\t}\n   332→\t\t// add dependencies on delegate virtual services\n   333→\t\tdelegates := ps.DelegateVirtualServicesConfigKey(listener.virtualServices)\n   334→\t\tfor _, delegate := range delegates {\n   335→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(delegate)\n   336→\t\t}\n   337→\n   338→\t\tmatchPort := needsPortMatch(listener)\n   339→\t\t// Infer more possible destinations from virtual services\n   340→\t\t// Services chosen here will not override services explicitly requested in listener.services.\n   341→\t\t// That way, if there is ambiguity around what hostname to pick, a user can specify the one they\n   342→\t\t// want in the hosts field, and the potentially random choice below won't matter\n   343→\t\tfor _, vs := range listener.virtualServices {\n   344→\t\t\tv := vs.Spec.(*networking.VirtualService)\n   345→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   346→\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.VirtualService,\n   347→\t\t\t\tName:      vs.Name,\n   348→\t\t\t\tNamespace: vs.Namespace,\n   349→\t\t\t})\n   350→\n   351→\t\t\tfor _, h := range virtualServiceDestinationHosts(v) {\n   352→\t\t\t\t// Default to this hostname in our config namespace\n   353→\t\t\t\tif s, ok := ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[host.Name(h)][configNamespace]; ok {\n   354→\t\t\t\t\t// This won't overwrite hostnames that have already been found eg because they were requested in hosts\n   355→\t\t\t\t\tvar vss *Service\n   356→\t\t\t\t\tif matchPort {\n   357→\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = serviceMatchingListenerPort(s, listener)\n   358→\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n   359→\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = s\n   360→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   361→\t\t\t\t\tif vss != nil {\n   362→\t\t\t\t\t\taddService(vss)\n   363→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   364→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   365→\n   366→\t\t\t\t\t// We couldn't find the hostname in our config namespace\n   367→\t\t\t\t\t// We have to pick one arbitrarily for now, so we'll pick the first namespace alphabetically\n   368→\t\t\t\t\t// TODO: could we choose services more intelligently based on their ports?\n   369→\t\t\t\t\tbyNamespace := ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[host.Name(h)]\n   370→\t\t\t\t\tif len(byNamespace) == 0 {\n   371→\t\t\t\t\t\t// This hostname isn't found anywhere\n   372→\t\t\t\t\t\tlog.Debugf(\"Could not find service hostname %s parsed from %s\", h, vs.Key())\n   373→\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   374→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   375→\n   376→\t\t\t\t\tns := This won't overwrite hostnames that have already been found eg because they were requested in hosts\n   386→\t\t\t\t\t\tvar vss *Service\n   387→\t\t\t\t\t\tif matchPort {\n   388→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = 407→\t\tout.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname] = s\n   408→\t\tif drList := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); drList != nil {\n   409→\t\t\tout.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = drList\n   410→\t\t\tfor _, dr := range drList {\n   411→\t\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   412→\t\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n   413→\t\t\t\t\tName:      dr.Name,\n   414→\t\t\t\t\tNamespace: dr.Namespace,\n   415→\t\t\t\t})\n   416→\t\t\t}\n   417→\t\t}\n   418→\t}\n   419→\n   420→\tif sidecar.OutboundTrafficPolicy == nil {\n   421→\t\tif 428→\t}\n   429→\n   430→\treturn out\n   431→}\n   432→\n   433→func convertIstioListenerToWrapper(ps *PushContext, configNamespace string,\n   434→\tistioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener) out.listenerHosts)\n   459→\n   460→\treturn out\n   461→}\n   462→\n   463→// GetEgressListenerForRDS returns the egress listener corresponding to\n   464→// the listener port or the bind address or the catch all listener\n   465→func (sc *SidecarScope) GetEgressListenerForRDS(port int, bind string) *IstioEgressListenerWrapper {\n   466→\tif sc == nil {\n   467→\t\treturn nil\n   468→\t}\n   469→\n   470→\tfor _, e := range sc.EgressListeners {\n   471→\t\t// We hit a catchall listener. This is the last listener in the list of listeners\n   472→\t\t// return as is\n   473→\t\tif e.IstioListener == nil || e.IstioListener.Port == nil {\n   474→\t\t\treturn e\n   475→\t\t}\n   476→\n   477→\t\t// Check if the ports match\n   478→\t\t// for unix domain sockets (i.e. port == 0), check if the bind is equal to the routeName\n   479→\t\tif int(e.IstioListener.Port.Number) == port {\n   480→\t\t\tif port == 0 { // unix domain socket\n   481→\t\t\t\tif e.IstioListener.Bind == bind {\n   482→\t\t\t\t\treturn e\n   483→\t\t\t\t}\n   484→\t\t\t\t// no match.. continue searching\n   485→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   486→\t\t\t}\n   487→\t\t\t// this is a non-zero port match\n   488→\t\t\treturn e\n   489→\t\t}\n   490→\t}\n   491→\n   492→\t// This should never be reached unless user explicitly set an empty array for egress\n   493→\t// listeners which we actually forbid\n   494→\treturn nil\n   495→}\n   496→\n   497→// HasIngressListener returns if the sidecar scope has ingress 538→\t_, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n   539→\treturn exists\n   540→}\n   541→\n   542→// AddConfigDependencies add extra config dependencies to this scope. This action should be done before the\n   543→// SidecarScope being used to avoid concurrent read/write.\n   544→func (sc *SidecarScope) AddConfigDependencies(dependencies ...ConfigKey) {\n   545→\tif *SidecarScope) DestinationRule(direction TrafficDirection, proxy *Proxy, svc host.Name) *config.Config {\n   559→\tdestinationRules := sc.destinationRules[svc]\n   560→\tvar catchAllDr *config.Config\n   561→\tfor _, destRule := range destinationRules {\n   562→\t\tdestinationRule := destRule.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n   563→\t\tif destinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == only for outbound configuration, because\n   568→\t\t// for inbound configuration, the settings at sidecar would be more explicit and the preferred way forward.\n   569→\t\tif sc.Namespace == destRule.Namespace &&\n   570→\t\t\tdestinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && direction == TrafficDirectionOutbound {\n   571→\t\t\tworkloadLabels := labels.Collection{proxy.Metadata.Labels}\n   572→\t\t\tworkloadSelector := labels.Instance(destinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n   573→\t\t\t// return destination rule if workload selector matches\n   574→\t\t\tif portion of the Sidecar config.\n   592→// Note that the returned service could be trimmed.\n   593→func (ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) selectServices(services []*Service, configNamespace string, hosts map[string][]host.Name) []*Service {\n   594→\timportedServices := make([]*Service, 0)\n   595→\twildcardHosts, wnsFound := hosts[wildcardNamespace]\n   596→\tfor _, s := range services {\n   597→\t\tconfigNamespace := s.Attributes.Namespace\n   598→\n   599→\t\t// Check if there is an explicit import of form ns/* or ns/host\n   600→\t\tif importedHosts, nsFound := hosts[configNamespace]; // Check if there is an import of form */host or */*\n   605→\t\t\tif svc := matchingService(wildcardHosts, s, ilw); svc != nil {\n   606→\t\t\t\timportedServices = append(importedServices, svc)\n   607→\t\t\t}\n   608→\t\t}\n   609→\t}\n   610→\n   611→\tvalidServices := make(map[host.Name]string)\n   612→\tfor _, svc := range importedServices {\n   613→\t\t_, f := validServices[svc.Hostname]\n in configNamespace, an arbitrary one will be chosen\n   617→\t\tif !f || svc.Attributes.Namespace == configNamespace {\n   618→\t\t\tvalidServices[svc.Hostname] = svc.Attributes.Namespace\n   619→\t\t}\n   620→\t}\n   621→\n   622→\tfilteredServices := make([]*Service, 0)\n   623→\t// Filter down to just instances in scope for the service\n   624→\tfor _, svc := range importedServices {\n 630→}\n   631→\n   632→// Return the original service or a trimmed service which has a subset of the ports in original service.\n   633→func matchingService(importedHosts []host.Name, service *Service, ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) *Service {\n   634→\tmatchPort := needsPortMatch(ilw)\n   635→\tfor _, importedHost := range importedHosts {\n   636→\t\t// Check if the hostnames match per usual hostname matching rules\n   637→\t\tif service.Hostname.SubsetOf(importedHost) {\n   638→\t\t\tif matchPort {\n   639→\t\t\t\treturn serviceMatchingListenerPort(service, ilw)\n   640→\t\t\t}\n   641→\t\t\treturn service\n   642→\t\t}\n   643→\t}\n   644→\treturn nil\n   645→}\n   646→\n   647→// serviceMatchingListenerPort constructs service with listener port.\n   648→func serviceMatchingListenerPort(service *Service, ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) *Service {\n   649→\tfor _, port := range service.Ports {\n   650→\t\tif port.Port == 657→}\n   658→\n   659→func needsPortMatch(ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) bool {\n   660→\t// If a listener is defined with a port, we should match services with port except in the following case.\n   661→\t//  - If Port's protocol is proxy protocol(HTTP_PROXY) in which case the egress listener is used as generic egress http proxy.\n   662→\treturn ilw.IstioListener != nil && Sidecar resource with some\n// preprocessed data to determine the list of services, virtualServices,\n// and destinationRules that are accessible to a given\n// sidecar. Precomputing the list of services, virtual services, dest rules\n// for a sidecar improves performance as we no longer need to compute this\n// list for every sidecar. We simply have to match a sidecar to a\n// SidecarScope. Note that this is not the same as public/private scoped\n// services. The list of services seen by every sidecar scope (namespace\n// wide or per workload) depends on the imports, the listeners, and other\n// settings.\n//\n// Every proxy workload of SidecarProxy type will always map to a\n// SidecarScope object. If the proxy's namespace does not have a user\n// specified Sidecar CRD, we will construct one that has a catch all egress\n// listener that imports every public service/virtualService in the mesh.\ntype SidecarScope struct {\n\tName string\n\t// This is the namespace where the sidecar takes effect,\n\t// maybe different from the ns where sidecar resides if sidecar is in root ns.\n\tNamespace string\n\t// The crd itself. Can be nil if we are constructing the default\n\t// sidecar scope\n\tSidecar *networking.Sidecar\n\n\t// Version this sidecar was computed for\n\tVersion string\n\n\t// Set of egress listeners, and their associated services.  A sidecar\n\t// scope should have either ingress/egress listeners or both.  For\n\t// every proxy workload that maps to a sidecar API object (or the\n\t// default object), we will go through every egress listener in the\n\t// object and process the Envoy listener or RDS based on the imported\n\t// services/virtual services in that listener.\n\tEgressListeners []*IstioEgressListenerWrapper\n\n\t// Union of services imported across all egress listeners for use by CDS code.\n\tservices           []*Service\n\tservicesByHostname map[host.Name]*Service\n\n\t// Destination rules imported across all egress listeners. This\n\t// contains the computed set based on public/private destination rules\n\t// as well as the inherited ones, in addition to the wildcard matches\n\t// such as *.com applying to foo.bar.com. Each hostname in this map\n\t// corresponds to a service in the services array above. When computing\n\t// CDS, we simply have to find the matching service and return the\n\t// destination rule.\n\tdestinationRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config\n\t// OutboundTrafficPolicy defines the outbound traffic policy for this sidecar.\n\t// If OutboundTrafficPolicy is ALLOW_ANY traffic to unknown destinations will\n\t// be forwarded.\n\tOutboundTrafficPolicy *networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy\n\n\t// Set of known configs this sidecar depends on.\n\t// This field will be used to determine the config/resource scope\n\t// which means which config changes will affect the proxies within this scope.\n\tconfigDependencies map[uint64]struct{}\n\n\t// The namespace to treat as the administrative root namespace for\n\t// Istio configuration.\n\t//\n\t// Changes to Sidecar resources in this namespace will trigger a push.\n\tRootNamespace string\n}\n\n// MarshalJSON implements json.Marshaller\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {\n\t// Json cannot expose unexported fields, so copy the ones we want here\n\treturn json.MarshalIndent(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"version\":               sc.Version,\n\t\t\"rootNamespace\":         sc.RootNamespace,\n\t\t\"name\":                  sc.Name,\n\t\t\"namespace\":             sc.Namespace,\n\t\t\"outboundTrafficPolicy\": sc.OutboundTrafficPolicy,\n\t\t\"services\":              sc.services,\n\t\t\"sidecar\":               sc.Sidecar,\n\t\t\"destinationRules\":      sc.destinationRules,\n\t}, \"\", \"  \")\n}\n\n// IstioEgressListenerWrapper is a wrapper for\n// networking.IstioEgressListener object. The wrapper provides performance\n// optimizations as it allows us to precompute and store the list of\n// services/virtualServices that apply to this listener.\ntype IstioEgressListenerWrapper struct {\n\t// The actual IstioEgressListener api object from the Config. It can be\n\t// nil if this is for the default sidecar scope.\n\tIstioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener\n\n\t// List of services imported by this egress listener above.\n\t// This will be used by LDS and RDS code when\n\t// building the set of virtual hosts or the tcp filterchain matches for\n\t// a given listener port. Two listeners, on user specified ports or\n\t// unix domain sockets could have completely different sets of\n\t// services. So a global list of services per sidecar scope will be\n\t// incorrect. Hence the per listener set of services.\n\tservices []*Service\n\n\t// List of virtual services imported by this egress listener above.\n\t// As with per listener services, this\n\t// will be used by RDS code to compute the virtual host configs for\n\t// http listeners, as well as by TCP/TLS filter code to compute the\n\t// service routing configs and the filter chain matches. We need a\n\t// virtualService set per listener and not one per sidecarScope because\n\t// each listener imports an independent set of virtual services.\n\t// Listener 1 could import a public virtual service for serviceA from\n\t// namespace A that has some path rewrite, while listener2 could import\n\t// a private virtual service for serviceA from the local namespace,\n\t// with a different path rewrite or no path rewrites.\n\tvirtualServices []config.Config\n\n\tlistenerHosts map[string][]host.Name\n}\n\nconst defaultSidecar = \"default-sidecar\"\n\n// DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace is a sidecar scope object with a default catch all egress listener\n// that matches the default Istio behavior: a sidecar has listeners for all services in the mesh\n// We use this scope when the user has not set any sidecar Config for a given config namespace.\nfunc DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps *PushContext, configNamespace string) *SidecarScope {\n\tdefaultEgressListener := &IstioEgressListenerWrapper{\n\t\tIstioListener: &networking.IstioEgressListener{\n\t\t\tHosts: []string{\"*/*\"},\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\tdefaultEgressListener.services = ps.servicesExportedToNamespace(configNamespace)\n\tdefaultEgressListener.virtualServices = ps.VirtualServicesForGateway(configNamespace, constants.IstioMeshGateway)\n\n\tout := &SidecarScope{\n\t\tName:               defaultSidecar,\n\t\tNamespace:          configNamespace,\n\t\tEgressListeners:    []*IstioEgressListenerWrapper{defaultEgressListener},\n\t\tservices:           defaultEgressListener.services,\n\t\tdestinationRules:   make(map[host.Name][]*config.Config),\n\t\tservicesByHostname: make(map[host.Name]*Service, len(defaultEgressListener.services)),\n\t\tconfigDependencies: make(map[uint64]struct{}),\n\t\tRootNamespace:      ps.Mesh.RootNamespace,\n\t\tVersion:            ps.PushVersion,\n\t}\n\n\t// Now that we have all the services that sidecars using this scope (in\n\t// this config namespace) will see, identify all the destinationRules\n\t// that these services need\n\tfor _, s := range out.services {\n\t\t// In some scenarios, there may be multiple Services defined for the same hostname due to ServiceEntry allowing\n\t\t// arbitrary hostnames. In these cases, we want to pick the first Service, which is the oldest. This ensures\n\t\t// newly created Services cannot take ownership unexpectedly.\n\t\t// However, the Service is from Kubernetes it should take precedence over ones not. This prevents someone from\n\t\t// \"domain squatting\" on the hostname before a Kubernetes Service is created.\n\t\t// This relies on the assumption that\n\t\tif existing, f := out.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname]; f &&\n\t\t\t!(existing.Attributes.ServiceRegistry != provider.Kubernetes && s.Attributes.ServiceRegistry == provider.Kubernetes) {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tout.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname] = s\n\t\tif dr := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); dr != nil {\n\t\t\tout.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = dr\n\t\t}\n\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n\t\t\tKind:      gvk.ServiceEntry,\n\t\t\tName:      string(s.Hostname),\n\t\t\tNamespace: s.Attributes.Namespace,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n\t\tfor _, dr := range drList {\n\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n\t\t\t\tName:      dr.Name,\n\t\t\t\tNamespace: dr.Namespace,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, el := range out.EgressListeners {\n\t\t// add dependencies on delegate virtual services\n\t\tdelegates := ps.DelegateVirtualServicesConfigKey(el.virtualServices)\n\t\tfor _, delegate := range delegates {\n\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(delegate)\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, vs := range el.virtualServices {\n\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.VirtualService,\n\t\t\t\tName:      vs.Name,\n\t\t\t\tNamespace: vs.Namespace,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy != nil {\n\t\tout.OutboundTrafficPolicy = &networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy{\n\t\t\tMode: networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy_Mode(ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy.Mode),\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn out\n}\n\n// ConvertToSidecarScope converts from Sidecar config to SidecarScope object\nfunc ConvertToSidecarScope(ps *PushContext, sidecarConfig *config.Config, configNamespace string) *SidecarScope {\n\tif sidecarConfig == nil {\n\t\treturn DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps, configNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\tsidecar := sidecarConfig.Spec.(*networking.Sidecar)\n\tout := &SidecarScope{\n\t\tName:               sidecarConfig.Name,\n\t\tNamespace:          configNamespace,\n\t\tSidecar:            sidecar,\n\t\tconfigDependencies: make(map[uint64]struct{}),\n\t\tRootNamespace:      ps.Mesh.RootNamespace,\n\t\tVersion:            ps.PushVersion,\n\t}\n\n\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n\t\tKind:      gvk.Sidecar,\n\t\tName:      sidecarConfig.Name,\n\t\tNamespace: sidecarConfig.Namespace,\n\t})\n\n\tegressConfigs := sidecar.Egress\n\t// If egress not set, setup a default listener\n\tif len(egressConfigs) == 0 {\n\t\tegressConfigs = append(egressConfigs, &networking.IstioEgressListener{Hosts: []string{\"*/*\"}})\n\t}\n\tout.EgressListeners = make([]*IstioEgressListenerWrapper, 0, len(egressConfigs))\n\tfor _, e := range egressConfigs {\n\t\tout.EgressListeners = append(out.EgressListeners,\n\t\t\tconvertIstioListenerToWrapper(ps, configNamespace, e))\n\t}\n\n\t// Now collect all the imported services across all egress listeners in\n\t// this sidecar crd. This is needed to generate CDS output\n\tout.services = make([]*Service, 0)\n\ttype serviceIndex struct {\n\t\tsvc   *Service\n\t\tindex int // index record the position of the svc in slice\n\t}\n\tservicesAdded := make(map[host.Name]serviceIndex)\n\taddService := func(s *Service) {\n\t\tif s == nil {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif foundSvc, found := servicesAdded[s.Hostname]; !found {\n\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.ServiceEntry,\n\t\t\t\tName:      string(s.Hostname),\n\t\t\t\tNamespace: s.Attributes.Namespace,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\tout.services = append(out.services, s)\n\t\t\tservicesAdded[s.Hostname] = serviceIndex{s, len(out.services) - 1}\n\t\t} else if foundSvc.svc.Attributes.Namespace == s.Attributes.Namespace && s.Ports != nil && len(s.Ports) > 0 {\n\t\t\t// merge the ports to service when each listener generates partial service\n\t\t\t// we only merge if the found service is in the same namespace as the one we're trying to add\n\t\t\tcopied := foundSvc.svc.DeepCopy()\n\t\t\tfor _, p := range s.Ports {\n\t\t\t\tfound := false\n\t\t\t\tfor _, osp := range copied.Ports {\n\t\t\t\t\tif p.Port == osp.Port {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tfound = true\n\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif !found {\n\t\t\t\t\tcopied.Ports = append(copied.Ports, p)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// replace service in slice\n\t\t\tout.services[foundSvc.index] = copied\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, listener := range out.EgressListeners {\n\t\t// First add the explicitly requested services, which take priority\n\t\tfor _, s := range listener.services {\n\t\t\taddService(s)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// add dependencies on delegate virtual services\n\t\tdelegates := ps.DelegateVirtualServicesConfigKey(listener.virtualServices)\n\t\tfor _, delegate := range delegates {\n\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(delegate)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmatchPort := needsPortMatch(listener)\n\t\t// Infer more possible destinations from virtual services\n\t\t// Services chosen here will not override services explicitly requested in listener.services.\n\t\t// That way, if there is ambiguity around what hostname to pick, a user can specify the one they\n\t\t// want in the hosts field, and the potentially random choice below won't matter\n\t\tfor _, vs := range listener.virtualServices {\n\t\t\tv := vs.Spec.(*networking.VirtualService)\n\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.VirtualService,\n\t\t\t\tName:      vs.Name,\n\t\t\t\tNamespace: vs.Namespace,\n\t\t\t})\n\n\t\t\tfor _, h := range virtualServiceDestinationHosts(v) {\n\t\t\t\t// Default to this hostname in our config namespace\n\t\t\t\tif s, ok := ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[host.Name(h)][configNamespace]; ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t// This won't overwrite hostnames that have already been found eg because they were requested in hosts\n\t\t\t\t\tvar vss *Service\n\t\t\t\t\tif matchPort {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = serviceMatchingListenerPort(s, listener)\n\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = s\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tif vss != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\taddService(vss)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// We couldn't find the hostname in our config namespace\n\t\t\t\t\t// We have to pick one arbitrarily for now, so we'll pick the first namespace alphabetically\n\t\t\t\t\t// TODO: could we choose services more intelligently based on their ports?\n\t\t\t\t\tbyNamespace := ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[host.Name(h)]\n\t\t\t\t\tif len(byNamespace) == 0 {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// This hostname isn't found anywhere\n\t\t\t\t\t\tlog.Debugf(\"Could not find service hostname %s parsed from %s\", h, vs.Key())\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tns := make([]string, 0, len(byNamespace))\n\t\t\t\t\tfor k := range byNamespace {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif ps.IsServiceVisible(byNamespace[k], configNamespace) {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tns = append(ns, k)\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tif len(ns) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tsort.Strings(ns)\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// Pick first namespace alphabetically\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// This won't overwrite hostnames that have already been found eg because they were requested in hosts\n\t\t\t\t\t\tvar vss *Service\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif matchPort {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = serviceMatchingListenerPort(byNamespace[ns[0]], listener)\n\t\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = byNamespace[ns[0]]\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif vss != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\taddService(vss)\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Now that we have all the services that sidecars using this scope (in\n\t// this config namespace) will see, identify all the destinationRules\n\t// that these services need\n\tout.servicesByHostname = make(map[host.Name]*Service, len(out.services))\n\tout.destinationRules = make(map[host.Name][]*config.Config)\n\tfor _, s := range out.services {\n\t\tout.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname] = s\n\t\tif drList := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); drList != nil {\n\t\t\tout.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = drList\n\t\t\tfor _, dr := range drList {\n\t\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n\t\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n\t\t\t\t\tName:      dr.Name,\n\t\t\t\t\tNamespace: dr.Namespace,\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif sidecar.OutboundTrafficPolicy == nil {\n\t\tif ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy != nil {\n\t\t\tout.OutboundTrafficPolicy = &networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy{\n\t\t\t\tMode: networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy_Mode(ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy.Mode),\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tout.OutboundTrafficPolicy = sidecar.OutboundTrafficPolicy\n\t}\n\n\treturn out\n}\n\nfunc convertIstioListenerToWrapper(ps *PushContext, configNamespace string,\n\tistioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener) *IstioEgressListenerWrapper {\n\tout := &IstioEgressListenerWrapper{\n\t\tIstioListener: istioListener,\n\t}\n\n\tout.listenerHosts = make(map[string][]host.Name)\n\tfor _, h := range istioListener.Hosts {\n\t\tparts := strings.SplitN(h, \"/\", 2)\n\t\tif len(parts) < 2 {\n\t\t\tlog.Errorf(\"Illegal host in sidecar resource: %s, host must be of form namespace/dnsName\", h)\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tif parts[0] == currentNamespace {\n\t\t\tparts[0] = configNamespace\n\t\t}\n\t\tif _, exists := out.listenerHosts[parts[0]]; !exists {\n\t\t\tout.listenerHosts[parts[0]] = make([]host.Name, 0)\n\t\t}\n\t\tout.listenerHosts[parts[0]] = append(out.listenerHosts[parts[0]], host.Name(parts[1]))\n\t}\n\n\tvses := ps.VirtualServicesForGateway(configNamespace, constants.IstioMeshGateway)\n\tout.virtualServices = SelectVirtualServices(vses, out.listenerHosts)\n\tsvces := ps.servicesExportedToNamespace(configNamespace)\n\tout.services = out.selectServices(svces, configNamespace, out.listenerHosts)\n\n\treturn out\n}\n\n// GetEgressListenerForRDS returns the egress listener corresponding to\n// the listener port or the bind address or the catch all listener\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) GetEgressListenerForRDS(port int, bind string) *IstioEgressListenerWrapper {\n\tif sc == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, e := range sc.EgressListeners {\n\t\t// We hit a catchall listener. This is the last listener in the list of listeners\n\t\t// return as is\n\t\tif e.IstioListener == nil || e.IstioListener.Port == nil {\n\t\t\treturn e\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Check if the ports match\n\t\t// for unix domain sockets (i.e. port == 0), check if the bind is equal to the routeName\n\t\tif int(e.IstioListener.Port.Number) == port {\n\t\t\tif port == 0 { // unix domain socket\n\t\t\t\tif e.IstioListener.Bind == bind {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn e\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t// no match.. continue searching\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// this is a non-zero port match\n\t\t\treturn e\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// This should never be reached unless user explicitly set an empty array for egress\n\t// listeners which we actually forbid\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// HasIngressListener returns if the sidecar scope has ingress listener set\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) HasIngressListener() bool {\n\tif sc == nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tif sc.Sidecar == nil || len(sc.Sidecar.Ingress) == 0 {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// Services returns the list of services imported by this egress listener\nfunc (ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) Services() []*Service {\n\treturn ilw.services\n}\n\n// VirtualServices returns the list of virtual services imported by this\n// egress listener\nfunc (ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) VirtualServices() []config.Config {\n\treturn ilw.virtualServices\n}\n\n// DependsOnConfig determines if the proxy depends on the given config.\n// Returns whether depends on this config or this kind of config is not scoped(unknown to be depended) here.\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) DependsOnConfig(config ConfigKey) bool {\n\tif sc == nil {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\n\t// This kind of config will trigger a change if made in the root namespace or the same namespace\n\tif _, f := clusterScopedConfigTypes[config.Kind]; f {\n\t\treturn config.Namespace == sc.RootNamespace || config.Namespace == sc.Namespace\n\t}\n\n\t// This kind of config is unknown to sidecarScope.\n\tif _, f := sidecarScopeKnownConfigTypes[config.Kind]; !f {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\n\t_, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n\treturn exists\n}\n\n// AddConfigDependencies add extra config dependencies to this scope. This action should be done before the\n// SidecarScope being used to avoid concurrent read/write.\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) AddConfigDependencies(dependencies ...ConfigKey) {\n\tif sc == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tif sc.configDependencies == nil {\n\t\tsc.configDependencies = make(map[uint64]struct{})\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, config := range dependencies {\n\t\tsc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n}\n\n// DestinationRule returns a destinationrule for a svc.\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) DestinationRule(direction TrafficDirection, proxy *Proxy, svc host.Name) *config.Config {\n\tdestinationRules := sc.destinationRules[svc]\n\tvar catchAllDr *config.Config\n\tfor _, destRule := range destinationRules {\n\t\tdestinationRule := destRule.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\t\tif destinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil {\n\t\t\tcatchAllDr = destRule\n\t\t}\n\t\t// filter DestinationRule based on workloadSelector for outbound configs.\n\t\t// WorkloadSelector configuration is honored only for outbound configuration, because\n\t\t// for inbound configuration, the settings at sidecar would be more explicit and the preferred way forward.\n\t\tif sc.Namespace == destRule.Namespace &&\n\t\t\tdestinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && direction == TrafficDirectionOutbound {\n\t\t\tworkloadLabels := labels.Collection{proxy.Metadata.Labels}\n\t\t\tworkloadSelector := labels.Instance(destinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n\t\t\t// return destination rule if workload selector matches\n\t\t\tif workloadLabels.IsSupersetOf(workloadSelector) {\n\t\t\t\treturn destRule\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\t// If there is no workload specific destinationRule, return the wild carded dr if present.\n\tif catchAllDr != nil {\n\t\treturn catchAllDr\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Services returns the list of services that are visible to a sidecar.\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) Services() []*Service {\n\treturn sc.services\n}\n\n// Return filtered services through the hosts field in the egress portion of the Sidecar config.\n// Note that the returned service could be trimmed.\nfunc (ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) selectServices(services []*Service, configNamespace string, hosts map[string][]host.Name) []*Service {\n\timportedServices := make([]*Service, 0)\n\twildcardHosts, wnsFound := hosts[wildcardNamespace]\n\tfor _, s := range services {\n\t\tconfigNamespace := s.Attributes.Namespace\n\n\t\t// Check if there is an explicit import of form ns/* or ns/host\n\t\tif importedHosts, nsFound := hosts[configNamespace]; nsFound {\n\t\t\tif svc := matchingService(importedHosts, s, ilw); svc != nil {\n\t\t\t\timportedServices = append(importedServices, svc)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if wnsFound { // Check if there is an import of form */host or */*\n\t\t\tif svc := matchingService(wildcardHosts, s, ilw); svc != nil {\n\t\t\t\timportedServices = append(importedServices, svc)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tvalidServices := make(map[host.Name]string)\n\tfor _, svc := range importedServices {\n\t\t_, f := validServices[svc.Hostname]\n\t\t// Select a single namespace for a given hostname.\n\t\t// If the same hostname is imported from multiple namespaces, pick the one in the configNamespace\n\t\t// If neither are in configNamespace, an arbitrary one will be chosen\n\t\tif !f || svc.Attributes.Namespace == configNamespace {\n\t\t\tvalidServices[svc.Hostname] = svc.Attributes.Namespace\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfilteredServices := make([]*Service, 0)\n\t// Filter down to just instances in scope for the service\n\tfor _, svc := range importedServices {\n\t\tif validServices[svc.Hostname] == svc.Attributes.Namespace {\n\t\t\tfilteredServices = append(filteredServices, svc)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn filteredServices\n}\n\n// Return the original service or a trimmed service which has a subset of the ports in original service.\nfunc {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01RqH3ty8i9HW2EY4BykbFtD","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01QxBhAhQbmNMUZGgLUVAhfi","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/logs/agent/investigation.md","content":"# Investigation Report: Stale Envoy Route Configuration After DestinationRule Update\n\n## Summary\n\nWhen multiple DestinationRules for the same host are merged during PushContext initialization, only the first DR's metadata (name/namespace) survives in the `consolidatedDestRules` structure. When a contributing DR is subsequently updated, the xDS push filter fails to recognize the dependency because the updated DR's ConfigKey is not registered in the SidecarScope's `configDependencies` map, causing the push to be silently skipped.\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause spans a three-component chain:\n\n1. **Metadata Loss During Merging** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go`, `mergeDestinationRule()` function)\n2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`, `AddConfigDependencies()` calls)\n3. **Dependency-Based Push Filtering** (`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go`, `checkProxyDependencies()` function)\n\nWhen two DestinationRules targeting the same host are merged, only one merged config object persists with the first DR's name/namespace. The second DR's identity is lost. Later, when dependency tracking occurs, only the first DR's ConfigKey is registered. When the second DR is updated, the update event carries the second DR's ConfigKey, which is not found in the dependency map, causing the push to be filtered out.\n\n---\n\n## Evidence\n\n### 1. Merging Logic Loses Metadata\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go`\n**Function:** `mergeDestinationRule()` (lines 38-109)\n\n**Problematic sequence (lines 41-104):**\n```go\nif mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n    addRuleToProcessedDestRules := true\n    for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n        existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n        // ... check if should merge ...\n\n        if bothWithoutSelector || (rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && selectorsMatch) {\n            addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false\n        }\n\n        // Deep copy destination rule, to prevent mutate it later when merge with a new one.\n        copied := mdr.DeepCopy()\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied  // Line 66: Updates existing at index i\n        mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\n        // Merge subsets and traffic policy into the FIRST DR's config...\n        for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n            if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n                mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n            }\n        }\n\n        if mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n            mergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n        }\n    }\n    if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {\n        // Line 102: Only appended if NO merge was performed\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Impact:** When two DRs without workload selectors exist for the same host:\n- The loop finds a matching DR (the first one)\n- `addRuleToProcessedDestRules` is set to false (line 60)\n- The FIRST DR is mutated with merged content from the SECOND DR (lines 77-93)\n- The SECOND DR is **not appended** to the list (line 102 skipped because `addRuleToProcessedDestRules` is false)\n- Result: `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` contains only **one config object** with the **first DR's metadata** but merged content from both DRs\n\n### 2. Consolidated Structure Stores Merged Configs Only\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n**Data Structure:** `consolidatedDestRules` (lines 251-256)\n\n```go\ntype consolidatedDestRules struct {\n    // Map of dest rule host to the list of namespaces to which this destination rule has been exported to\n    exportTo map[host.Name]map[visibility.Instance]bool\n    // Map of dest rule host and the merged destination rules for that host\n    destRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config  // Line 255: List of configs, but only ONE per merged group\n}\n```\n\nWhen `SetDestinationRules()` processes configs via `mergeDestinationRule()`, the resulting `destRules` map contains merged configs, losing the identity of contributing DRs.\n\n### 3. Dependency Registration Only Covers Merged Configs\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`\n**Function:** `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` (lines 173-251)\n\n**Critical section (lines 209-211, 219-227):**\n```go\n// Line 209: Fetches merged configs from PushContext\nif dr := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); dr != nil {\n    out.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = dr  // Line 210: dr is a list of MERGED configs\n}\n\n// Lines 219-227: Iterate over merged configs ONLY\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,           // Line 223: MERGED config's name\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,      // Line 224: MERGED config's namespace\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Similar code in `ConvertToSidecarScope()`** (lines 408-418):\n```go\nif drList := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); drList != nil {\n    out.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = drList\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,      // Only the FIRST (merged) DR's name\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace, // Only the FIRST (merged) DR's namespace\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Impact:** When a service depends on merged DRs, only the first DR's ConfigKey is registered. The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `configDependencies`.\n\n### 4. destinationRule() Method Returns Merged Configs\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n**Function:** `destinationRule()` (lines 990-1066)\n\n**Key lines (1010, 1020, 1043, 1050):**\n```go\n// Returns from consolidatedDestRules.destRules[hostname]\nreturn ps.destinationRuleIndex.namespaceLocal[proxyNameSpace].destRules[hostname]  // Line 1010\nreturn ps.destinationRuleIndex.rootNamespaceLocal.destRules[hostname]               // Line 1020\nreturn out  // from getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace                           // Line 1043\nreturn out  // from getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace                           // Line 1050\n```\n\nAll code paths return the merged configs from `consolidatedDestRules.destRules`, which contains only one config per merged group.\n\n### 5. The map only contains the hash of `ConfigKey{..., Name: \"reviews-traffic-policy\", ...}`. The lookup returns `false`.\n\n8. **Result:** `ConfigAffectsProxy()` returns `false` → `DefaultProxyNeedsPush()` returns `false` → `PushProcess()` in `ads.go` (line 688) skips the push → Envoy sidecar never receives the updated DR-2 configuration.\n\n---\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Fix Strategy\n\nThe root cause must be addressed at the point where metadata is lost: **the merging phase**. There are two high-level approaches:\n\n#### Option A: Preserve All Contributing DR Metadata (Recommended)\n\nModify `mergeDestinationRule()` to **retain all contributing DRs** in the `destRules` list with their original metadata intact. Instead of merging into a single config, keep both configs but establish a logical relationship:\n\n1. **Change `consolidatedDestRules` data structure** to track both:\n   - Individual DR metadata (name/namespace of each contributing DR)\n   - Merged routing content (consolidated subsets, traffic policies)\n\n2. **Modify `mergeDestinationRule()`** to:\n   - Append both DRs to `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` instead of merging into one\n   - Mark or annotate which configs are merged and with what others\n   - Ensure subsets and traffic policies are properly deduplicated but attributed to their sources\n\n3. **Update dependency registration** in `sidecar.go` to iterate over ALL contributing DRs, not just the merged config.\n\n#### Option B: Map Merged DRs Back to Sources\n\nCreate a metadata map in `consolidatedDestRules` that tracks:\n- Which DRs contributed to each merged config\n- A reverse mapping from individual DR's ConfigKey to the merged config's position\n\nThen, during dependency registration, iterate over both the merged configs AND their contributing sources.\n\n#### Option C: Defer Merging Until After Dependency Registration\n\nMove the merging phase to after SidecarScope initialization, so dependency registration happens on individual, unmerged DRs.\n\n### Diagnostic Steps\n\nTo verify the issue in a live cluster:\n\n1. **Check the sidecar scope dependencies:**\n   ```bash\n   # On Istiod, add debug logging to SidecarScope.AddConfigDependencies()\n   # Check which DR ConfigKeys are registered\n   ```\n\n2. **Monitor config updates:**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch Pilot logs for:\n   # - When a contributing DR is subsequently updated, the xDS push filter fails to recognize the dependency because the updated DR's ConfigKey is not registered in the SidecarScope's `configDependencies` map, causing the push to be silently skipped.\n\n---\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause spans a three-component chain:\n\n1. **Metadata Loss During Merging** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go`, `mergeDestinationRule()` function)\n2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`, `AddConfigDependencies()` calls)\n3. **Dependency-Based Push Filtering** (`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go`, `checkProxyDependencies()` function)\n\nWhen two DestinationRules targeting the same host are merged, only one merged config object persists with the first DR's name/namespace. The second DR's identity is lost. Later, when dependency tracking occurs, only the first DR's ConfigKey is registered. When the second DR is updated, the update event carries the second DR's ConfigKey, which is not found in the dependency map, causing the push to be filtered out.\n\n---\n\n## Evidence\n\n### 1. Merging Logic Loses Metadata\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go`\n**Function:** `mergeDestinationRule()` (lines 38-109)\n\n**Problematic sequence (lines 41-104):**\n```go\nif mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n    addRuleToProcessedDestRules := true\n    for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n        existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n        // ... check if should merge ...\n\n        if bothWithoutSelector || (rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && selectorsMatch) {\n            addRuleToProcessedDestRules = false\n        }\n\n        // Deep copy destination rule, to prevent mutate it later when merge with a new one.\n        copied := mdr.DeepCopy()\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied  // Line 66: Updates existing at index i\n        mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n\n        // Merge subsets and traffic policy into the FIRST DR's config...\n        for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n            if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n                mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n            }\n        }\n\n        if mergedRule.TrafficPolicy == nil && rule.TrafficPolicy != nil {\n            mergedRule.TrafficPolicy = rule.TrafficPolicy\n        }\n    }\n    if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {\n        // Line 102: Only appended if NO merge was performed\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Impact:** When two DRs without workload selectors exist for the same host:\n- The loop finds a matching DR (the first one)\n- `addRuleToProcessedDestRules` is set to false (line 60)\n- The FIRST DR is mutated with merged content from the SECOND DR (lines 77-93)\n- The SECOND DR is **not appended** to the list (line 102 skipped because `addRuleToProcessedDestRules` is false)\n- Result: `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` contains only **one config object** with the **first DR's metadata** but merged content from both DRs\n\n### 2. Consolidated Structure Stores Merged Configs Only\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n**Data Structure:** `consolidatedDestRules` (lines 251-256)\n\n```go\ntype consolidatedDestRules struct {\n    // Map of dest rule host to the list of namespaces to which this destination rule has been exported to\n    exportTo map[host.Name]map[visibility.Instance]bool\n    // Map of dest rule host and the merged destination rules for that host\n    destRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config  // Line 255: List of configs, but only ONE per merged group\n}\n```\n\nWhen `SetDestinationRules()` processes configs via `mergeDestinationRule()`, the resulting `destRules` map contains merged configs, losing the identity of contributing DRs.\n\n### 3. Dependency Registration Only Covers Merged Configs\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`\n**Function:** `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` (lines 173-251)\n\n**Critical section (lines 209-211, 219-227):**\n```go\n// Line 209: Fetches merged configs from PushContext\nif dr := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); dr != nil {\n    out.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = dr  // Line 210: dr is a list of MERGED configs\n}\n\n// Lines 219-227: Iterate over merged configs ONLY\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,           // Line 223: MERGED config's name\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,      // Line 224: MERGED config's namespace\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Similar code in `ConvertToSidecarScope()`** (lines 408-418):\n```go\nif drList := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); drList != nil {\n    out.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = drList\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,      // Only the FIRST (merged) DR's name\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace, // Only the FIRST (merged) DR's namespace\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Impact:** When a service depends on merged DRs, only the first DR's ConfigKey is registered. The second DR's ConfigKey is never added to `configDependencies`.\n\n### 4. destinationRule() Method Returns Merged Configs\n\n**File:** `/workspace/pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n**Function:** `destinationRule()` (lines 990-1066)\n\n**Key lines (1010, 1020, 1043, 1050):**\n```go\n// Returns from consolidatedDestRules.destRules[hostname]\nreturn ps.destinationRuleIndex.namespaceLocal[proxyNameSpace].destRules[hostname]  // Line 1010\nreturn ps.destinationRuleIndex.rootNamespaceLocal.destRules[hostname]               // Line 1020\nreturn out  // from getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace                           // Line 1043\nreturn out  // from getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace                           // Line 1050\n```\n\nAll code paths return the merged configs from `consolidatedDestRules.destRules`, which contains only one config per merged group.\n\n### 5.
